. /*==================================================
> project:       Create 400 bins in each dataset of LIS repository
> Author:        R.Andres Castaneda Aguilar 
> E-email:       acastanedaa@worldbank.org
> url:           
> Dependencies:  The World Bank
> ----------------------------------------------------
> Creation Date:    11 Dec 2019 - 20:53:13
> Modification Date: Oct 19 2022  
> Do-file version:    01
> References:          
> Output:             
> ==================================================*/
. /*==================================================
>               0: Program set up
> ==================================================*/
.  
. //------------To modify
. *local silc   "at be cz dk ee fi fr de gr hu is ie it lt lu nl no pl ro rs sk si es se ch uk"    // 26 EUSILC countries
. *local nosilc "au br ca cl cn co do eg ge gt in il ci jp ml mx ps pa py pe ru za kr tw us uy vn" // 27 rest
. local silc   ""

. local nosilc "us"

. /* 
> local surveys "us13 us16 de15 de16 il16 il14"
> local y = substr("`surveys'", 3,.)
> local year "20`y'"
> local surveys: subinstr local surveys " " "h ", all
> local surveys "`surveys'h"
> */
. //------------Do NOT modify
. local countries "`silc' `nosilc'"

. numlist "2001/2022"

. local years = "`r(numlist)'"

. foreach year of loca years {
  2.  local y = substr("`year'", 3,.)
  3.  local ys "`ys' `y'"
  4. }

. foreach c of local countries {
  2.  foreach y of local ys {
  3.  local surveys "`surveys' `c'`y'h"
  4.  }
  5. }

. /*==================================================
>               1: Program to calculate 400 bins
> ==================================================*/
. cap program drop _nq

. discard

. program define _nq, rclass
  1. syntax varname [fweight pweight/] ///
>                 [if/] [in] [, ///
>                 BY(varlist) ///
>                 NQ(string)  ///
>                 nvar(string) ///
>                 ]
  2. qui {
  3.  // Weigths
.  tempvar wgt
  4.  if ("`weight'" == "") {
  5.  gen `wgt' = 1
  6.  }
  7.  else {
  8.  gen `wgt' = `exp'
  9.  }
 10.  
.  // calculations
.  
.  tempvar a b c
 11.  
.  sort `varlist' `wgt', stable
 12.  gen `a' = sum(`wgt')           // cummulative sum
 13.  sum `wgt'                      // total number of people
 14.  gen double `b' = `a'/`r(sum)'  // cummalitve share of population
 15.  gen double `c' = `b'*`nq'      // rescale share of population by number of bins
 16.  gen long `nvar' = ceil(`c')    // round to ceil integer
 17.  replace `nvar' = `nq' if `nvar' > `nq'  // replace to top of number of bins just in case
 18.  
.  gen one = 1
 19.  
.  noi table `nvar'  [`weight' = `wgt'], c(sum one mean `varlist'  min `varlist' max `varlist')  /* 
>   */ left concise format(%16.5f)
 20.  
. }
 21. end

. /*==================================================
>         2:  Loop over surveys
> ==================================================*/
. foreach x of local surveys {
  2.  cap {
  3.  use ${`x'}, clear
  4.  
.  local iso  = upper(iso3[1])
  5.  local year = year[1]
  6.  local wave = wave[1]
  7.  local currency : label currency `=currency[1]'
  8.  keep hid  dhi hpopwgt nhhmem 
  9.  gen double popw=hpopwgt*nhhmem 
 10.  gen double lcu_pc = (dhi/nhhmem) // leave it annual per capita
 11.  drop if (lcu_pc < 0 | lcu_pc >= . | popw >= .)
 12.  }
 13.  if (_rc) continue
 14.  
.  noi mata: printf("##1 `iso' `year' `wave'\n")
 15.  noi mata: printf("##2 `currency'\n")
 16.  _nq lcu_pc [pw = popw], nq(400) nvar(nq)
 17. }
##1 USA 2001 5
##2 [840]USD - US Dollar
